INNER JOIN [Tag] AS [pt.Tag] ON [p.Tags].[TagId] = [pt.Tag].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p0].[Id]
    FROM [Post] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Category] AS [p.Category0] ON [p0].[CategoryId] = [p.Category0].[Id]
    WHERE [p0].[Id] = @__id_0
    ORDER BY [p0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p.Tags].[PostId] = [t].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]
